<script>
    // Override click events on inline links for the topbar-button, this will give
    // us smooth scrolling effect.
    $(document).on('click', '.topbar-button a[href^="#"]', function(e) {

        // the cheapest page only on the first page
        if (FaresFilter.search_filters.page != 1) {
            FaresFilter.paginateTo(1);
        }

        if ($('#myContent input:checkbox:not(:checked)').length &gt; 0) {
            // reset the filters
            FaresFilter.resetAllFilters();
        }

        // target element id
        var id = $(this).attr('href');

        // target element
        var $id = $(id);
        if ($id.length === 0) {
            return;
        }

        // prevent standard hash navigation (avoid blinking in IE)
        e.preventDefault();

        // top position relative to the document (include some padding for the "Top Seller" banner)
        var pos = $id.offset().top - $('#fare_avg_price_banner div:first').outerHeight();

        // animated top scrolling
        $('body, html').animate({scrollTop: pos });
    });

    function initTooltip() {
        var tooltip = new Tooltip({
            trigger: '.trigger',
            container: '.tooltip',
            width: 300
        });
        tooltip.show();
    }

        var payload = {"type":"roundtrip","seg0_from":"YUL","seg0_to":"CWB","seg0_date":"2018-12-11","seg1_date":"2018-12-25","seg1_from_code":"YUL","seg2_from_code":"YUL","seg3_from_code":"YUL","seg4_from_code":"YUL","num_adults":"1","num_children":"0","num_infants":"0","num_infants_lap":"0","seat_class":"Economy","seg1_from":"CWB","seg1_to":"YUL","campaign":"1","search_id":"81b68b249dcb5e09a55fea4bedaac660","flexible_search_id":"81b68b249dcb5e09a55fea4bedaac660"};
    $.ajax({
        method: 'POST',
        url: '/flight/fare-avg-price/banner',
        dataType : 'json',
        data: payload,
        success: function (data) {
            if (data.result) {
                $('#fare_avg_price_banner').html(data.html.banner).show().find('div:first').slideDown('slow');
                initTooltip();
            }
        }
    });
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {

        $('a.mobile-menu-show').on('click', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            e.stopPropagation();
            slideDiv('.nav-container', 'slide-trigger');
        });

        $('#trigger-language-dd').on('click', function (e) {
            if (window._gaTracker) {
                window._gaTracker('send', {
                    hitType: 'event',
                    eventCategory: 'Interactions',
                    eventAction: 'Language Menu Opened'
                });
            }
        });

        $('#header_lang a').on('click', function (e) {
            if (window._gaTracker) {
                window._gaTracker('send', {
                    hitType: 'event',
                    eventCategory: 'Interactions',
                    eventAction: 'Language Menu Selected: ' + e.target.text.trim()
                });
            }
        });
    });
    
    function saveEvent(controller)
    {
        if (window._gaTracker) {
            window._gaTracker('send', {
                hitType: 'event',
                eventCategory: 'Interactions',
                eventAction: 'FareAlertPlus Menu Selected: ' + controller
            });
            return false;
        }
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    
    (function ($) {

        if (typeof window.idleModalFareAlert === 'undefined') {
            window.idleModalFareAlert = $('#fare-alert-idle').clone();
        }

        var idleDisplayed = $.cookie('idle-displayed') === "true";
        var timer = 0;
        var seconds = 60;
        var idleInterval = setInterval(function(){
            timer++;

            if (timer === seconds) {
                if (!idleDisplayed) {
                    Modal.open({html: window.idleModalFareAlert.html(), width: 500, unclosable: false});

                    if ($('#fare-alert-idle:visible')) {
                        $('#fare-alert-idle').remove();
                    }

                    $.cookie('idle-displayed', true, { expires: 1 });
                    idleDisplayed = true;
                }
                clearInterval(idleInterval);
            }
        }, 1000);

        $(window).on('mousemove keydown touchmove', function() {
            timer = 0;
        });
        
    })(jQuery);
    
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
  $('.buttons-add-remove').click(function (e) {
    !$('.seg1').is(':visible') ?
      ($('.buttons-add-remove-right').closest('li').hide(), $('.buttons-add-remove-right').hide()) :
      ($('.buttons-add-remove-right').closest('li').fadeIn(100), $('.buttons-add-remove-right').fadeIn(100));
    $('.seg4').is(':visible') ?
      ($('.buttons-add-remove-left').closest('li').hide(), $('.buttons-add-remove-left').hide()) :
      ($('.buttons-add-remove-left').closest('li').fadeIn(100), $('.buttons-add-remove-left').fadeIn(100));
  });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var flightsearch = {};
    var current_trip_type;
    var formContainerSelector = '.hp-form';
    
    $(document).ready(function(){
        
        flightsearch = new FlightSearch({

            'form_view_type' : 'home'
        });

        flightsearch.init();

        $('.flight_type_button_v2').each(function(){
            $(this).on('click', function(){
                current_trip_type = $(this).data('flightType');
                flightsearch.changeFlightTypeTab('' + current_trip_type, true, true);
                $('#validation_errors').slideUp();
            });

        });
        
                $('.btn-fhub-submit').on('click', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            trackCabinClassGA();

            var button = this;
            var locale = $('#btn-submit-locale').val();

            $(button).html(locale);
            flightsearch.submit();
        });
        
        // Add/Remove Segments
        $('.buttons-add-remove a').on('click', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            flightsearch.multiSegmentAddRemove($(this).data('option'));
        });
        
        // Tabs
        $('input:visible').each(function (index) {
            
            $(this).attr('tabindex', index + 1);
            
        });

        $('input[name^=seg]').on('click', function () {

            var input = this;
            if ($(input).val().length &gt;= 1) {
                $(input).select();
                $(input).focus();
            }
        });

                $(window).bind('pageshow', function(event) {
            if (event.originalEvent.persisted) {
                window.location.reload()
            }
        });
        
    });

    /**
     * Track the Cabin Class with respective to/from destinations of each segment and send to Google Analytics
     */
    function trackCabinClassGA()
    {
        var airportSegment = "";
        var homeSeatNode =  $('#home-seat-class').val();

        for (var i = 0; i &lt; 5; i++) {
            var inputSegmentFrom = $("input[name=seg" + i + "_from_code]");
            var inputSegmentTo = $("input[name=seg" + i + "_to_code]");

            if (inputSegmentFrom.attr('value') &amp;&amp; inputSegmentTo.attr('value')) {
                airportSegment += inputSegmentFrom.attr('value') + "-" + inputSegmentTo.attr('value')+ " / ";
            }
        }

        if (homeSeatNode) {
            sendEventToGA({category: 'Interaction', action: 'Cabin Class Selected: ' + homeSeatNode, label: airportSegment});
        }
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

    if (FaresFilter.landing_times_shown)
    {
        toggleInfo($('#landing_toggle'), '#toggleLanding', 'smaller', 'Show landing times', true);
    }

    if (FaresFilter.departure_zones_shown)
    {
        $('#cp0_departure_zones_title').toggle();

        toggleInfo($('#departure_zone_toggle'), '.departure_zones', 'smaller', 'Show more', true);
    }

    var widget_values = {"stops":[],"carriers":{"JJ":{"name":"LATAM Airlines Brazil","code":"JJ","price":981.01},"multi":{"name":"Multiple Airlines","code":"multi","price":981.01},"CM":{"name":"Copa Airlines","code":"CM","price":1302.1},"AA":{"name":"American Airlines","code":"AA","price":1695.37},"DL":{"name":"Delta","code":"DL","price":1720.17},"UA":{"name":"United","code":"UA","price":1987.44},"LA":{"name":"LATAM Airlines","code":"LA","price":2118.01},"AC":{"name":"Air Canada","code":"AC","price":2249.29},"AM":{"name":"Aeromexico","code":"AM","price":2279.09},"LX":{"name":"Swiss","code":"LX","price":12520.65}},"min_duration":"","max_duration":"","layover_airports":[],"total_city_pairs":"","departure_zones":[],"arrival_zones":[],"search_airports":{"origin":{"city_code":"YMQ","YUL":{"name":"Pierre Elliott Trudeau International","price":981.01}},"destination":{"city_code":"CWB","CWB":{"name":"Afonso Pena International Airport","price":981.01}}},"departure_zones_one_step":[[1,2,3],[1,2,3]],"arrival_zones_one_step":[[0,1,2,3],[1,2,3]],"layover_airpors_one_step":[],"max_duration_one_step":355740,"min_duration_one_step":122880,"stops_one_step":{"2":981.01},"layover_airports_one_step":{"GRU":"Sao Paulo","YYZ":"Toronto","JFK":"New York","PTY":"Panama City","LGA":"New York","MIA":"Miami","YTZ":"Toronto","IAD":"Washington","MEX":"Mexico City","GIG":"Rio De Janeiro","BOS":"Boston","EWR":"Newark","CGH":"Sao Paulo","ATL":"Atlanta","IAH":"Houston","DFW":"Dallas-fort Worth","ORD":"Chicago","YHM":"Hamilton","VCP":"Campinas","DCA":"Washington","POA":"Porto Alegre","ZRH":"Zurich"},"order_by":"price","order_direction":"ASC","page":1,"longer_trips":1,"codeshare_dupes":0,"show_red_eye":1};
    FaresFilter.initSliders(widget_values);
    FaresFilter.initSearchFilters(widget_values);

    function toggleLanding(elem)
    {
        FaresFilter.landing_times_shown = !FaresFilter.landing_times_shown;

        toggleInfo(elem, '#toggleLanding', 'smaller', 'Show landing times', true);
    }

    function toggleDepartureTimes(elem)
    {
        FaresFilter.departure_zones_shown = !FaresFilter.departure_zones_shown;

        //$('#cp0_departure_zones_title').toggle();

        toggleInfo(elem, '.departure_zones', 'smaller', 'Show more', true);
    }

    initializeTipsy('.filter-sidebar', 'south-west');

    /**
     * Persist the div state after filtering
     * 
     * @param element
     * @param targetId
     * @param faresFilterAttribute
     */
    function persistToggleDiv(element, targetId, faresFilterAttribute)
    {
        var domElement = $(element),
            domTarget = $('#' + targetId);
        var label = null;

        if (domTarget.is(':visible')) {
            FaresFilter[faresFilterAttribute] = false;
            domElement.removeClass('expanded').addClass('collapsed');
            domTarget.slideToggle();
            label = 'collapsed';
        } else {
            FaresFilter[faresFilterAttribute] = true;
            domElement.addClass('expanded').removeClass('collapsed');
            domTarget.slideToggle();
            label = 'expanded';
        }
        var action = targetId == 'more_filters' ? 'Filters' : 'Airports';
        sendEventToGA({category: 'Filter Interaction', action: action + ' option', label: label});
    }

    function checkboxSelectAll(event, input)
    {
        var domInput = $(input);

        if (domInput.attr('id') == 'checkboxSelectAllAirlines') {
            if ($('[name="carrier"]:checked').length == $('[name="carrier"]').length) {
                FaresFilter.checkAllCarriers('none');
                return;
            } else {
                FaresFilter.checkAllCarriers('all');
                return;
            }
        }

        if (domInput.attr('id') == 'checkboxSelectAllLayoverAirports') {
            if ($('[name="layover-airport"]:checked').length == $('[name="layover-airport"]').length) {
                event.preventDefault();
                return;
            } else {
                FaresFilter.checkAllLayoverAirports('all');
                return;
            }
        }
    };

    (function() {
        // persist toggle divs when filtering
        if (FaresFilter.isExpandedAdditionalOptions) {
            $('#more_filters').show();
            $('.more-filter.slide-toggle-button').addClass('expanded').removeClass('collapsed');
        }
        if (FaresFilter.isExpandedAirlines) {
            $('#toggle_airlines').show();
            $('.more-airlines.slide-toggle-button').addClass('expanded').removeClass('collapsed');
        }

        // manage check all inputs
        if ($('[name="carrier"]:checked').length == $('[name="carrier"]').length) {
            $('#checkboxSelectAllAirlines').prop('checked', true);
        }
        if ($('[name="layover-airport"]:checked').length == $('[name="layover-airport"]').length) {
            $('#checkboxSelectAllLayoverAirports').prop('checked', true);
        }

        // add extra behavior to checkboxes
        $('[name="carrier"], .airlines-filter a.pointer').on('click', function() {
            setTimeout(function(){
                if ($('[name="carrier"]:checked').length == $('[name="carrier"]').length) {
                    $('#checkboxSelectAllAirlines').prop('checked', true);
                } else {
                    $('#checkboxSelectAllAirlines').prop('checked', false);
                }
            }, 10);
        });
        $('[name="layover-airport"], .layover_airports a.pointer').on('click', function() {
            setTimeout(function(){
                if ($('[name="layover-airport"]:checked').length == $('[name="layover-airport"]').length) {
                    $('#checkboxSelectAllLayoverAirports').prop('checked', true);
                } else {
                    $('#checkboxSelectAllLayoverAirports').prop('checked', false);
                }
            }, 10);
        });
    })();

    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">

    $(document).ready(function () {

        $('.amatrix-buttons-middle li a').each(function () {

            $(this).on('click', function (e) {
                
                e.preventDefault();
                var airline = $(this);
                
                // Remove class + add to this
                $('.amatrix-buttons-middle li a').removeClass('active');
                $(this).addClass('active');
                $('a.amatrix-clear').css('color', '#4d96b3');
                
                FaresFilter.onlyCarrier($(airline).data('carrier'));
            });

        });
        
        var matrixItemWidth = 0;
        var matrixContainerStart = 0;
        var matrixContainerEnd = 0;
        var matrixListStart = 0;
        var matrixListEnd = 0;
        var moveCarousel = 0;
        var numSlides = 3;
        
        
        $('button.scroller').on('click', function () {

            var btn = $(this);
            var matrixContainer = $('.amatrix-buttons-middle');
            var matrixList = $('.amatrix-list');
            var matrixItem = $('.amatrix-item');
            
            matrixItemWidth = matrixItem.outerWidth();
            matrixContainerStart = matrixContainer.offset().left;
            matrixContainerEnd = matrixContainerStart + matrixContainer.width();
            matrixListStart = matrixList.offset().left;
            matrixListEnd = matrixListStart + matrixList.width();
            

            if (btn.hasClass('nav-next')) {
                if (matrixListEnd &gt; matrixContainerEnd) {
                    moveCarousel +=  matrixItemWidth * numSlides;
                    matrixContainer.stop(false, false).animate({ scrollLeft: moveCarousel });
                }
            } else if (btn.hasClass('nav-prev')) {
                if (matrixContainerStart &gt; matrixListStart) {
                    moveCarousel -=  matrixItemWidth * numSlides;
                    matrixContainer.stop(false, false).animate({ scrollLeft: moveCarousel });
                }
            }
            
        });
        
        $('a.amatrix-close').on('click', function (e) {
           
            e.preventDefault();
            $('.amatrix-wrap').fadeOut(200);
            
        });
        
        $('a.amatrix-clear').on('click', function (e) {
           
            e.preventDefault();
            $('.amatrix-buttons-middle li a').removeClass('active');
            $(this).css('color', '#999');
            FaresFilter.checkAllCarriers('all');
            
        });
        
    });

</script> </div>

    $(function () {
        $('.phone-modal-trigger').on('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            _gaq.push(["_trackEvent",'Interaction','Phone Banner','Search Results: Opened',,1]);_gaTracker('send', {"hitType":"event","eventCategory":"Interaction","eventAction":"Phone Banner","eventLabel":"Search Results: Opened","nonInteraction":true});            Modal.open({html:$('#phone-deals-modal').html(), width:500, position: 'fixed', 'top': 200});
        });
    });
</script> <script type="text/javascript">
        (function($) {
            
            if (typeof window.packageFareAlert === 'undefined') {
                window.packageFareAlert = $('#fare-alert-package').clone();
            }
            
            $('.price-alert-btn').on('click', function(e){
                
                e.preventDefault();
                Modal.open({html:  window.packageFareAlert.html(), width:500, unclosable:false});
                
                if ($('#fare-alert-package:visible')) {
                    $('#fare-alert-package').remove();
                }
                $('input[name="flight-package"]').val($(this).data('pid'));
                _gaq.push(["_trackEvent",'Interaction','Clicked Fare Alerts Button','Search Results: Opened (Standard)',,0]);_gaTracker('send', {"hitType":"event","eventCategory":"Interaction","eventAction":"Clicked Fare Alerts Button","eventLabel":"Search Results: Opened (Standard)","nonInteraction":0});                
            })
        })(jQuery);
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">

    var long_flights_txt = FaresFilter.longer_trips_shown ? 'Hide Longer Flights' : 'Show All';
    $('#toggle_long_flights').html(long_flights_txt);

    
        //Show/Hide flexible dates matrix on results load
        if (!FaresFilter.flexible_matix_shown)                  
        {
            $('#fares-search-flexible').hide();
            $('#fares-search-top-flights-buttons a[order=flexible_dates]').removeClass('active');        
        }
        else
        {
            $('#fares-search-top-flights-buttons a[order=flexible_dates]').addClass('active');
        }

    //Hover effect on the SELECT button
    $('.container-package-select-btn').on('touchend', function(e) {
        eval($(this).attr('onclick'));
    });
    
    $('.container-package-select-btn,.container-package').mouseover(function(){
        $(this).parents('li').find('.flight-info-checkbox').css('visibility', 'visible');
        $(this).parents('li').find('.flightDetails').css('visibility', 'visible');
        $(this).parents('li').find('.package-row-middle').css('background-color', 'transparent');
        $(this).parents('li').find('.package-row-bottom').css('background-color', 'transparent');
        $(this).parents('li').find('.ac2u-select').css('visibility', 'visible');
    });
    
    $('.container-package-select-btn,.container-package, .tipsy').mouseout(function(){
        $(this).parents('li').find('.flight-info-checkbox').css('visibility', 'hidden');    
        $(this).parents('li').find('.flightDetails').css('visibility', 'hidden');
        $(this).parents('li').find('.package-row-middle').css('background-color', 'transparent');
        $(this).parents('li').find('.package-row-bottom').css('background-color', 'transparent');
        $(this).parents('li').find('.ac2u-select').css('visibility', 'hidden');
        
        //if specific flights filter is selected, dont hide the checkbox
        $(this).parents('li').find('input[name=specific-flights-checkbox]:checked').css('visibility', 'visible');
    });

    initializeTipsy('#fares-search-results', 'south-east');
    initializeTipsy('#fares-search-results', 'south-west');
    initializeTipsy('#fares-search-results', 'north-east');
    initializeTipsy('#fares-search-results', 'north-west');
    initializeTipsy('#fares-search-results', 'north');
    initializeTipsy('#fares-search-results', 'south'); 

</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    
    // Fare family clicks
    $('.exp-ac2u-select.seg0 a').click(function() {

        $parent_node = $('.exp-ac2u-select.seg0');

        $parent_node.find('a[rel='+$(this).attr('rel')+']').removeClass('active');
        $(this).addClass('active');
        
        //change the total price
        var package_id = $(this).attr('pid');
        var currency_symbol = $(this).attr('cr');
        var num_pax = $(this).attr('pax');
        var pax_types = $(this).attr('pax_types');
        var original_package_id = $(this).attr('original_pid');
        var cp = $(this).attr('cp');
        var nonachtotal = $(this).attr('nonachtotal');
        
        var pax_array = pax_types.split(',');
        
        var pax_prices = [];
        
        // initialize prices for all passengers
        for (var i=0; i&lt;pax_array.length; i++)
        {
            var pax_type = pax_array[i];
            
            pax_prices[pax_type] = [];
            pax_prices[pax_type]['base'] = 0;
            pax_prices[pax_type]['tax'] = 0;
            pax_prices[pax_type]['total'] = 0;
        }
        
        // calculate package price
        var package_price = 0;

        // for 2 city pairs
        for (var i = 0; i &lt; 2; i++)
        {
            if ($('.exp-ac2u-select.seg' + i).find('a.active[rel='+package_id+i+']').length)
            {
                var active_fare = $('.exp-ac2u-select.seg' + i).find('a.active[rel='+package_id+i+']');
                
                package_price = parseFloat(package_price) +  parseFloat($(active_fare).attr('price'));
                
                // change the details modal
                $('.'+original_package_id+'_'+cp+'_cabin').html($(active_fare).attr('fare'));
                
                // add passenger prices
                for (var j=0; j&lt;pax_array.length; j++)
                {
                    var pax_type = pax_array[j];
                    
                    pax_prices[pax_type]['base'] = parseFloat(pax_prices[pax_type]['base']) + parseFloat($(active_fare).attr(pax_type+'_base'));
                    pax_prices[pax_type]['tax'] = parseFloat(pax_prices[pax_type]['tax']) + parseFloat($(active_fare).attr(pax_type+'_tax'));
                    pax_prices[pax_type]['total'] = parseFloat(pax_prices[pax_type]['total']) + parseFloat($(active_fare).attr(pax_type+'_total'));
                }
            }
        }

        /******** BROCK HERE **********/
        package_price = 0;
        if ($('.exp-ac2u-select.seg0').find('a.active[rel='+package_id+'0'+']').length) {
            package_price += parseFloat($('.exp-ac2u-select.seg0').find('a.active[rel='+package_id+'0'+']').attr('price'));
        } else {
            package_price += parseFloat(nonachtotal);
        }
        if ($('.exp-ac2u-select.seg1').find('a.active[rel='+package_id+'0'+']').length) {
            package_price += parseFloat($('.exp-ac2u-select.seg1').find('a.active[rel='+package_id+'0'+']').attr('price'));
        } else {
            package_price += parseFloat(nonachtotal);
        }
        /******** BROCK HERE **********/
        
        // change the details container
        $('.'+original_package_id+'_total_price').html(currency_symbol+parseFloat(package_price).toFixed(2));
        
        for (var i=0; i&lt;pax_array.length; i++)
        {
            var pax_type = pax_array[i];
            
            $('.'+original_package_id+'_'+pax_type+'_total').html(currency_symbol+parseFloat(pax_prices[pax_type]['total']).toFixed(2));
            $('.'+original_package_id+'_'+pax_type+'_base').html(currency_symbol+parseFloat(pax_prices[pax_type]['base']).toFixed(2));
            $('.'+original_package_id+'_'+pax_type+'_tax').html(currency_symbol+parseFloat(pax_prices[pax_type]['tax']).toFixed(2));
        }
        
        // use updated fare option if present
        if ($(this).attr('updated_price'))
        {
            package_price = $(this).attr('updated_price');
        }
        
        // calculate average per passenger
        package_price = parseFloat(package_price)/parseInt(num_pax);

        var whole = parseFloat(package_price).toFixed(2).split('.')[0],
            fraction = parseFloat(package_price).toFixed(2).split('.')[1];

        $('[data-package-id="'+package_id+'_price"]').find('.price-whole').html(whole);
        $('[data-package-id="'+package_id+'_price"]').find('.price-fraction').html(fraction);
    });

    $('.exp-ac2u-select.seg1 a').click(function() {

        $parent_node = $('.exp-ac2u-select.seg1');

        $parent_node.find('a[rel='+$(this).attr('rel')+']').removeClass('active');
        $(this).addClass('active');

        //change the total price
        var package_id = $(this).attr('pid');
        var currency_symbol = $(this).attr('cr');
        var num_pax = $(this).attr('pax');
        var pax_types = $(this).attr('pax_types');
        var original_package_id = $(this).attr('original_pid');
        var cp = $(this).attr('cp');
        var nonachtotal = $(this).attr('nonachtotal');

        var pax_array = pax_types.split(',');

        var pax_prices = [];

        // initialize prices for all passengers
        for (var i=0; i&lt;pax_array.length; i++)
        {
            var pax_type = pax_array[i];

            pax_prices[pax_type] = [];
            pax_prices[pax_type]['base'] = 0;
            pax_prices[pax_type]['tax'] = 0;
            pax_prices[pax_type]['total'] = 0;
        }

        // calculate package price
        var package_price = 0;

        // for 2 city pairs
        for (var i = 0; i &lt; 2; i++)
        {
            if ($('.exp-ac2u-select.seg' + i).find('a.active[rel='+package_id+i+']').length)
            {
                var active_fare = $('.exp-ac2u-select.seg' + i).find('a.active[rel='+package_id+i+']');

                package_price = parseFloat(package_price) +  parseFloat($(active_fare).attr('price'));

                // change the details modal
                $('.'+original_package_id+'_'+cp+'_cabin').html($(active_fare).attr('fare'));

                // add passenger prices
                for (var j=0; j&lt;pax_array.length; j++)
                {
                    var pax_type = pax_array[j];

                    pax_prices[pax_type]['base'] = parseFloat(pax_prices[pax_type]['base']) + parseFloat($(active_fare).attr(pax_type+'_base'));
                    pax_prices[pax_type]['tax'] = parseFloat(pax_prices[pax_type]['tax']) + parseFloat($(active_fare).attr(pax_type+'_tax'));
                    pax_prices[pax_type]['total'] = parseFloat(pax_prices[pax_type]['total']) + parseFloat($(active_fare).attr(pax_type+'_total'));
                }
            }
        }

        /******** BROCK HERE **********/
        package_price = 0;
        if ($('.exp-ac2u-select.seg0').find('a.active[rel='+package_id+'0'+']').length) {
            package_price += parseFloat($('.exp-ac2u-select.seg0').find('a.active[rel='+package_id+'0'+']').attr('price'));
        } else {
            package_price += parseFloat(nonachtotal);
        }

        if ($('.exp-ac2u-select.seg1').find('a.active[rel='+package_id+'0'+']').length) {
            package_price += parseFloat($('.exp-ac2u-select.seg1').find('a.active[rel='+package_id+'0'+']').attr('price'));
        } else {
            package_price += parseFloat(nonachtotal);
        }
        /******** BROCK HERE **********/

        // change the details container
        $('.'+original_package_id+'_total_price').html(currency_symbol+parseFloat(package_price).toFixed(2));

        for (var i=0; i&lt;pax_array.length; i++)
        {
            var pax_type = pax_array[i];

            $('.'+original_package_id+'_'+pax_type+'_total').html(currency_symbol+parseFloat(pax_prices[pax_type]['total']).toFixed(2));
            $('.'+original_package_id+'_'+pax_type+'_base').html(currency_symbol+parseFloat(pax_prices[pax_type]['base']).toFixed(2));
            $('.'+original_package_id+'_'+pax_type+'_tax').html(currency_symbol+parseFloat(pax_prices[pax_type]['tax']).toFixed(2));
        }

        // use updated fare option if present
        if ($(this).attr('updated_price'))
        {
            package_price = $(this).attr('updated_price');
        }

        // calculate average per passenger
        package_price = parseFloat(package_price)/parseInt(num_pax);

        var whole = parseFloat(package_price).toFixed(2).split('.')[0],
            fraction = parseFloat(package_price).toFixed(2).split('.')[1];

        $('[data-package-id="'+package_id+'_price"]').find('.price-whole').html(whole);
        $('[data-package-id="'+package_id+'_price"]').find('.price-fraction').html(fraction);
    });
    
    
    // Update AC Package with selected fare families
    function updatePackage(package_id, caller)
    {
        var selected_fare = [];

        var first_fare_family = $('.exp-ac2u-select.seg0').find('a.active[original_pid='+package_id+']');
        var second_fare_family = $('.exp-ac2u-select.seg1').find('a.active[original_pid='+package_id+']');

        if (first_fare_family.length) {
            selected_fare[0] = first_fare_family.attr('fare_key');
        } else {
            selected_fare[0] = "";
        }
        if (second_fare_family.length) {
            selected_fare[1] = second_fare_family.attr('fare_key');
        } else {
            selected_fare[1] = "";
        }

        var params = {
            search_id : '81b68b249dcb5e09a55fea4bedaac660',
            package_id : package_id,
            selected_fare_families : selected_fare
        };

        if (selected_fare.length)
        {
            // make request to update package with selected fare families
            $.ajax({
                url: 'https://www.flighthub.com//flight/ac-update',
                cache: false,
                data: params,
                method: 'post',
                success: function(data){
                    if (data.result)
                    {
                        window.location.href = 'https://www.flighthub.com/checkout/billing/flight/81b68b249dcb5e09a55fea4bedaac660/'+package_id;
                    }
                },
                error: function(xhr, status, error){
                }
            });                
        }
    }

    
    var redirect_base_url = 'https://www.flighthub.com/flight/search?type=roundtrip&amp;seg0_from=YUL&amp;seg0_to=CWB&amp;seg0_date=2018-12-11&amp;seg1_date=2018-12-25&amp;seg1_from_code=YUL&amp;seg2_from_code=YUL&amp;seg3_from_code=YUL&amp;seg4_from_code=YUL&amp;num_adults=1&amp;num_children=0&amp;num_infants=0&amp;num_infants_lap=0&amp;seat_class=Economy&amp;seg1_from=CWB&amp;seg1_to=YUL&amp;campaign=1&amp;search_id=81b68b249dcb5e09a55fea4bedaac660&amp;flexible_search_id=81b68b249dcb5e09a55fea4bedaac660';
    
    /**
    * Redirects to the inbound flights for given outbound flight
    * Called on the SELECT of outbound ACH packages
    */
    function showInboundFlights(package_id)
    {
        showLoadingResults();
        
        var fare_key = $('#fares-search-package-list').find('a.active[pid='+package_id+']').attr('fare_key');
        
        redirect_url = redirect_base_url+'&amp;selected_pids[0]='+package_id+'&amp;selected_fare_option='+fare_key;
        
        // redirect to inbound flights page
        window.location.href = redirect_url;
    }

</script></div>

<script type="text/javascript">

  function ffButtonHover (el) {
    if($(el).hasClass('ff-ipad-btn')) {
      if($(el).prev('.tooltip-test-text').css('visibility') === 'visible'){
        $(el).prev('.tooltip-test-text').css('visibility', 'hidden');
      } else {
        $(el).prev('.tooltip-test-text').css('visibility', 'visible');
      }
    }
  };

  $('.buttons-add-remove').click(function (e) {
    !$('.seg1').is(':visible') ?

  /**
 * Handler for the airlines matrix
 *  - should not alter the sidebar filters
 *  - use different post params to filter the packages
 */
AirlinesMatrixFilters = {
    airlinesMatrixContainer: '#airlines_matrix_container',
    matrixOverflowContainer: '.matrix-overflow',
    matrixList: '.airline-matrix-list',
    matrixItem: '.matrix-item',
    matrixItemOption: 'a.matrix-carrier-wrap, a.matrix-price',
    dismissMatrixButton: '.dismiss-matrix',
    modalContainer: '#loading_filter',
    packageListContainer: '#fares-search-results',
    cookieName: 'search_dismissed_airlines_matrix',
    showAllFaresButton: '.show-all-fares',
    paginationContainer: '.container-paging .airline-matrix-pagination',
    airlinesMatrixFilters: {},
    
    init: function (partialHtml) {
        var self = this;

        if (typeof partialHtml === 'string' &amp;&amp; partialHtml.length &gt; 0) {
            self.setContent(partialHtml);
        }
        
        // it has no content so far, wait for the _loading_js.php response
        if (!self._hasContent()) {
            return;
        }

        // if it has content but the user already dismissed the matrix since last 24 hours
        if (self._userIsCookied()) {
            $(self.airlinesMatrixContainer).hide();
            return;
        }

        // start it
        self._setDefaultAirlinesMatrixFilters();
        self._setLocalListeners();
        self._setGlobalListeners();
    },

    /**
     * User is cookied?
     */
    _userIsCookied: function() {
        var self = this;
        
        return $.cookie(self.cookieName);
    },
    
    /**
     * Check if the matrix already has content
     *
     * @returns {boolean}
     */
    _hasContent: function() {
        return $(this.matrixOverflowContainer).find(this.matrixItem).length &gt; 0;
    },

    /**
     * Apply the partial content and restart the component
     *
     * @param partialHtml Partial _airlines_matrix.php
     */
    setContent: function(partialHtml) {
        $(this.airlinesMatrixContainer).html(partialHtml);
        this.init();
    },

    /**
     * Default post data params
     */
    _setDefaultAirlinesMatrixFilters: function() {
        this.airlinesMatrixFilters = {
            'search_id': '81b68b249dcb5e09a55fea4bedaac660',
            'carriers': 'all',
            'segment_stops': 'all',
            'multi': false,
            'page': '1'
        }
    },

    /**
     * Set listeners to global events
     */
    _setGlobalListeners: function() {
        var self = this;
        
        $('body').on('beforeSidebarFilteringPackages', function(){
            self.resetAirlinesMatrixFilters();
        });
    },

    /**
     * Add listener for the airline matrix elements.
     */
    _setLocalListeners: function () {
        var self = this,
            body = $('body'),
            matrixItemWidth = null,
            moveCarousel = 0,
            numSlides = 2,
            matrixContainerStart = 0,
            matrixContainerEnd = 0,
            matrixListStart = 0,
            matrixListEnd = 0;

        var container = $(self.airlinesMatrixContainer);

        // handle matrix cell click
        container.find(self.matrixItemOption).on('click', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();

            var currentItemOption = $(this);

            var airline = $(this),
                data = airline.data(),
                params;

            if (!data) {
                return;
            }

            self._activateMatrixItem(currentItemOption);
            self._activateAllShowAllFaresButtons();

            // set post data parameters
            params = self.airlinesMatrixFilters;
            params.carriers = data.carrier;
            params.segment_stops = data.numStops;
            params.multi = data.multi;
            params.page = '1';

            // filter the packages list by carrier
            self.filter(params);
        });


        // handle the slide (arrow button)
        body.find('.matrix-btn').on('click', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();

            var theBtn = $(this),
                matrixContainer = $(self.matrixOverflowContainer),
                matrixList = $(self.matrixList),
                matrixItem = $(self.matrixItemOption);

            if (matrixContainer.length === 0) {
                return;
            }

            matrixItemWidth = matrixItem.outerWidth();

            matrixContainerStart = matrixContainer.offset().left;
            matrixContainerEnd = matrixContainerStart + matrixContainer.width();

            matrixListStart = matrixList.offset().left;
            matrixListEnd = matrixListStart + matrixList.width();

            if (theBtn.hasClass('nav-next')) {
                if (matrixListEnd &gt; matrixContainerEnd) {
                    moveCarousel +=  matrixItemWidth * numSlides;
                    matrixContainer.stop(false, false).animate({ scrollLeft: moveCarousel });
                }
            } else if (theBtn.hasClass('nav-prev')) {
                if (matrixContainerStart &gt; matrixListStart) {
                    moveCarousel -=  matrixItemWidth * numSlides;
                    matrixContainer.stop(false, false).animate({ scrollLeft: moveCarousel });
                }
            }
        });

        // close the airline matrix
        $(self.dismissMatrixButton).on('click', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();

            $(self.airlinesMatrixContainer).slideUp(400, function() {
                $.cookie(self.cookieName, 1, { expires: 1 });    
            });
        });

        $(self.showAllFaresButton).on('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            self.resetAirlinesMatrixFilters();
            self.filter(self.airlinesMatrixFilters);
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            self.timeout = setTimeout(function () {
                var matrixContainer = $(self.matrixOverflowContainer),
                    matrixList = $(self.matrixList);

                if (matrixContainer.length === 0) {
                    return;
                }
                matrixContainerStart = matrixContainer.offset().left;
                matrixContainerEnd = matrixContainerStart + matrixContainer.width();

                matrixListStart = matrixList.offset().left;
                matrixListEnd = matrixListStart + matrixList.width();
            }, 300);
        });
    },

    /**
     * parameters validator
     *
     * @returns {boolean}
     */
    _isAirlinesMatrixFiltersValid: function () {
        return this.airlinesMatrixFilters.search_id !== ''
                    &amp;&amp; this.airlinesMatrixFilters.carriers !== ''
                    &amp;&amp; this.airlinesMatrixFilters.segment_stops !== '';
    },

    /**
     * post parameters setter
     *
     * @param {object} post_data
     */
    _setAirlinesMatrixFilters: function (post_data) {

        this.airlinesMatrixFilters = {
            'search_id' : post_data.search_id,
            'carriers' : post_data.carriers,
            'segment_stops' : post_data.segment_stops,
            'multi' : post_data.multi,
            'page' : post_data.page
        };

    },

    /**
     * Deactivate visually all items
     */
    _deactivateAllMatrixItems: function() {
        $(this.airlinesMatrixContainer).find(this.matrixItem).removeClass('active');
        $(this.airlinesMatrixContainer).find(this.matrixItemOption).removeClass('active');
    },

    /**
     * Activate a matrix item
     */
    _activateMatrixItem: function (currentMatrixItemOption) {
        var currentMatrixItem = $(currentMatrixItemOption).parents(this.matrixItem);

        this._deactivateAllMatrixItems();

        $(currentMatrixItem).addClass('active');
        $(currentMatrixItemOption).addClass('active');
    },

    _deactivateAllShowAllFaresButtons: function() {
        $(this.airlinesMatrixContainer).find(this.showAllFaresButton).addClass('disabled');
    },

    _activateAllShowAllFaresButtons: function() {
        $(this.airlinesMatrixContainer).find(this.showAllFaresButton).removeClass('disabled');
    },

    /**
     * Handle the xhr _request
     * - load the packages list filtered by carrier
     * - load the pagination for the list above
     * - set the active carrier
     */
    _request: function () {

        if (!this._isAirlinesMatrixFiltersValid()) {
            return;
        }

        var self = this,
            params = self.airlinesMatrixFilters,
            modalContainer = $(self.modalContainer),
            body = $('body');

        if (FaresFilter.asyncFiltering) {
            if (FaresFilter.xhr &amp;&amp; FaresFilter.xhr.readyState &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; FaresFilter.xhr.readyState &lt; 4 ) {
                FaresFilter.xhr.abort();
            }
        } else {
            Modal.open({
                html: modalContainer.html(),
                width: modalContainer.css('width'),
                height: modalContainer.css('height'),
                unclosable: true
            });
        }

        FaresFilter.xhr = $.ajax({
            type: 'POST',
            url: 'https://www.flighthub.com/flight/filter-by-airlines-matrix',
            data: params,
            beforeSend: function() {
                body.triggerHandler('beforeFilteringPackages');
                body.triggerHandler('beforeAirlinesMatrixFilteringPackages');

                if (FaresFilter.asyncFiltering) {
                    FaresFilter.domFlightsResultsWrap.addClass('filtering');
                }
            },
            success: function(response) {
                var paddingTop = 10;

                if (!response.result) {
                    return;
                }

                $(self.packageListContainer).hide().html(response.html.results).fadeIn(200);

                $('html, body').animate({
                    scrollTop: $(self.airlinesMatrixContainer).offset().top - paddingTop
                }, 500);
            }
        }).always(function() {
            body.triggerHandler('filteredPackages');
            body.triggerHandler('airlinesMatrixFilteredPackages');

            if (FaresFilter.asyncFiltering) {
                FaresFilter.domFlightsResultsWrap.removeClass('filtering');
            } else {
                Modal.close();
            }
        });
    },

    /**
     * Get content
     * 
     * @param {object} post_data
     */
    filter: function (postData) {
        var self = this;

        this._setAirlinesMatrixFilters(postData);

        if (FaresFilter.asyncFiltering) {
            FaresFilter.domFlightsResultsWrap.addClass('filtering');

            clearTimeout(FaresFilter.asyncFilteringTimeout);

            FaresFilter.asyncFilteringTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
                self._request();
            }, FaresFilter.asyncFilteringBuffer);
        } else {
            this._request();
        }
    },

    /**
     * Paginate the content.
     * 
     * @param page
     */
    paginate: function (page) {
        this.airlinesMatrixFilters.page = page;
        this._request();
    },

    /**
     * Deactivate all matrix items
     */
    resetAirlinesMatrixFilters: function () {
        // reset the post data
        this._setDefaultAirlinesMatrixFilters();

        // reset visually
        this._deactivateAllShowAllFaresButtons();
        this._deactivateAllMatrixItems();
    }
};  FaresFilter.init('flight', {"type":"roundtrip","seg0_from":"YUL","seg0_to":"CWB","seg0_date":"2018-12-11","seg1_date":"2018-12-25","seg1_from_code":"YUL","seg2_from_code":"YUL","seg3_from_code":"YUL","seg4_from_code":"YUL","num_adults":"1","num_children":"0","num_infants":"0","num_infants_lap":"0","seat_class":"Economy","seg1_from":"CWB","seg1_to":"YUL","campaign":"1","search_id":"81b68b249dcb5e09a55fea4bedaac660","flexible_search_id":"81b68b249dcb5e09a55fea4bedaac660"}, '81b68b249dcb5e09a55fea4bedaac660', '81b68b249dcb5e09a55fea4bedaac660', [], '');

  $('#fares-search-content').on("click", "ul *:not(.exp-details, .exp-details *)", function (event) {
    event.stopPropagation();
    // dont toggle details for SELECT button click and Fare Alert buttons
    if (!$(this).hasClass('button-select-fare')
      &amp;&amp; !$(this).hasClass('mobile-details')
      &amp;&amp; !$(this).hasClass('package-alerts')
    ) {
      if ($(this).is('li')) {
        showFlightDetails($(this).attr('pid'));
      }
      else {
        showFlightDetails($(this).parents('li').attr('pid'));
      }
    }
  });
  $(document).ready(function () {
      activateToggleableTooltips();
    $("#cmn-toggle-4").on("click", function () {
      porterToggle(this);
    });
    $(".porter-ad-wrap").on("click", function () {
      var toggleElement = $("#cmn-toggle-4");

      if (status === "PD") {
        $(".switch input").prop("checked", true);

        $(".switch input").removeAttr("checked");

    });

  });
  function porterToggle(element) {
    var status = $(element).attr("data-show");
    var changeTextDiv = $(".show-text");
    if (status == "PD") {
      $(element).attr("data-show", "all");
      FaresFilter.onlyCarrier("PD");
      changeTextDiv.html("Show All Flights");
    } else {
      $(element).attr("data-show", "PD");
      FaresFilter.checkAllCarriers("all");
      changeTextDiv.html("Show Porter Flights");
    }
  }

      height: $('#loading_results').css('height'),
      unclosable: true
    });
    return true;
  }

  }
  // Fare alert email
  // this GET vparameter comes from one of the lander pages
  var fare_alert_email = '';
  var search_id = '81b68b249dcb5e09a55fea4bedaac660';
  var interval = setInterval(setEmail, 5000);
  // promises to chain an event based on out of order events.
  var flexDatePostRenderPromise = $.Deferred(),
    phoneBannerAjaxPromise = $.Deferred(),
    phoneBannerDisplayPromise = $.when(flexDatePostRenderPromise, phoneBannerAjaxPromise);
  function setEmail() {
    if ((fare_alert_email != '') &amp;&amp; (search_id != '')) {
      $.ajax({
        url: 'https://www.flighthub.com/flight/create-alert/' + search_id + '/' + fare_alert_email,
        dataType: 'json',
        type: 'GET',
        success: function (data) {
          clearInterval(interval);
                    },
        error: function (status) {
          clearInterval(interval);
        }
      });
    }
  }

  //start flex date stuff
  </script>

        BottomAlert = {
    typeSearch: 'search',
    typeBooking: 'booking',
    typeSellingOutQuickly: 'selling-out-quickly',
    showSearchAlertWhenMoreThan: 1,                                     // 150
    showBookingsAlertWhenMoreThan: 50,                                  // 50
    showAfterLoadingModalDelay: 3,                                      // delay after loading modal is closed
    showSellingOutQuicklyAlertDelaySeconds: 4,                          // show x seconds after the regular alerts
    showAlertForSeconds: 10,                                            // alerts duration
    showAlertsAfterSeconds: 0,                                          // show alerts delay after the page loads
    domContainer: '#bottomAlert',
    isLoadingPackages: 0,

    init: function ()
    {
        var self = this;

        window.showBottomAlerts = false;

        $(document).ready(function () {
            if (self.isLoadingPackages === 0) {
                // if it's a page refresh, allow the alerts right away
                self.allowAlerts();
            } else if (self.isLoadingPackages === 1 &amp;&amp; typeof FareLoader !== 'undefined'){
                // if it's still loading listen the body waiting for it
                $('body').on('fareLoadingFinished', function() {
                    window.setTimeout(
                        function () {
                            self.allowAlerts();
                        },
                        self.showAfterLoadingModalDelay * 1000
                    );
                })
            } else {
                // something went wrong... show the alerts anyways
                self.allowAlerts();
            }

            self._initLastSearchesAlert();
        });
    },

    _initLastSearchesAlert: function ()
    {
        var self = this;

        return $.ajax({
            type: 'GET',
            url: 'https://www.flighthub.com/flight/get-alert-searches?to_airport_code=CWB',
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function (data) {
                if (data.amount &gt;= self.showSearchAlertWhenMoreThan) {
                    data.type = self.typeSearch;

                    self._showAlert(data);
                    self._initSellingOutQuicklyAlert();
                }
            }
        });
    },

    _initLastBookingsAlert: function ()
    {
        var self = this;

        return $.ajax({
            type: 'GET',
            url: 'https://www.flighthub.com/flight/get-alert-bookings?to_airport_code=CWB',
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function (data) {
                if (data.amount &gt;= self.showBookingsAlertWhenMoreThan) {
                    data.type = self.typeBooking;

                    self._showAlert(data);
                }
            }
        });
    },

    _initSellingOutQuicklyAlert: function ()
    {
        var self = this;

        return $.ajax({
            type: 'GET',
            url: 'https://www.flighthub.com/flight/get-alert-selling-out-quickly?to_airport_code=CWB&amp;date=2018-12-11&amp;num_adults=1&amp;num_children=0&amp;num_infants=0&amp;num_infants_lap=0',
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function (data) {
                data.type = self.typeSellingOutQuickly;
                data.delay = self.showSellingOutQuicklyAlertDelaySeconds;

                self._showAlert(data);
            }
        });
    },

    /**
     * Manage the flag `window.showBottomAlerts`.
     */
    allowAlerts: function ()
    {
        var self = this;


        window.setTimeout(
            function () {
                window.showBottomAlerts = true;
            },
            self.showAlertsAfterSeconds * 1000
        );
    },

    /**
     * Check the flag `window.showBottomAlerts`. If it's allowed, show the alerts.
     * Otherwise, try again in X seconds.
     */
    _showAlert: function (data)
    {
        var self = this;

        if (window.showBottomAlerts) {
            var delay,
                domCurrentAlert = $(self.domContainer + ' .item-' + data.type);

            // set the alert content
            domCurrentAlert.find('.data-city').html(data.city);
            domCurrentAlert.find('.data-amount').html(data.amount);
            domCurrentAlert.find('.data-date').html(data.date);

            // show the alert
            delay = typeof data.delay === 'undefined'
                ? 0
                : data.delay;

            window.setTimeout(
                function () {
                    domCurrentAlert.addClass('active');
                },
                delay * 1000
            );

            // bind the close button
            $('.btn-close').on('click', function () {
                $(this).closest('.item').removeClass('active');
            });

            // show alert for x seconds
            window.setTimeout(
                function () {
                    domCurrentAlert.removeClass('active');
                },
                (self.showAlertForSeconds + delay) * 1000
            );
        } else {
            // check again if it's allowed to show the alert in X seconds
            window.setTimeout(
                function () {
                    self._showAlert(data);
                },
                1000
            );
        }
    }
};        BottomAlert.init();
    </script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    OnboardingSteps = {
    domBody: $('body'),
    domSteps: undefined,
    domCloseButton: undefined,
    cookieLastSeen: 'onboarding_last_seen',
    cookieDismissedName: 'onboarding_dismissed',

    init: function()
    {
        this._setDomObjects();

        if (this._isEligibleForOnboarding()) {
            this._bindDomObjects();
            this._showStep(this._getLastSeen());
        }
    },

    _setDomObjects: function()
    {
        this.domSteps = $('[data-component="OnboardingSteps"][data-name="domSteps"]');
        this.domCloseButton = $('[data-component="OnboardingSteps"][data-name="domCloseButton"]');
    },

    _bindDomObjects: function()
    {
        var self = this;

        this.domCloseButton.on('click', function() {
            self._dismissOnboarding();
        });

        this.domBody.on('fareLoadingFinished', function() {
            self.init();
        });
    },

    _isEligibleForOnboarding: function()
    {
        return $.cookie(this.cookieDismissedName) ? $.cookie(this.cookieName) : true;
    },

    _dismissOnboarding: function()
    {
        this.domBody.triggerHandler('dismissedOnboarding');
        this._hideStep('all');
        $.cookie(this.cookieDismissedName, true, { expires: 365 });
    },

    _hideStep: function(step)
    {
        if (step == 'all') {
            this.domSteps.fadeOut(100);
        } else {
            this._getDomStep(step).fadeOut(100);
        }
    },
    
    _showStep: function(step)
    {
        if (step == 0) {
            step = 1
        }

        var domStep = this._getDomStep(step);

        if (typeof domStep == 'undefined') {
            return;
        }

        this._setLastSeen(step);
        domStep.fadeIn(100);
    },

    _getLastSeen: function()
    {
        return $.cookie(this.cookieLastSeen) ? parseInt($.cookie(this.cookieLastSeen)) : 0;
    },

    _setLastSeen: function(step)
    {
        $.cookie(this.cookieLastSeen, step, { expires: 365});
    },

    _getDomStep: function(step)
    {
        var domStep;

        this.domSteps.each(function() {
            var domThis = $(this);

            if (domThis.data('step') == step) {
                domStep = domThis;
            }
        });

        return domStep;
    }
};    OnboardingSteps.init();
</script>

        function fareAlertSubscribe(id) {

      var parentContainerId = '#' + id;
      var emailInputId = parentContainerId + ' input.fare-alert-email';
      var fareAlert = new FareAlert(
        {
          emailInput: emailInputId,
          confirmButton: parentContainerId + ' button.fare-alert-btn',
          outputContainer: parentContainerId + ' div.fa-output-container'
        }
      );
      var payload = {"type":"roundtrip","seg0_from":"YUL","seg0_to":"CWB","seg0_date":"2018-12-11","seg1_date":"2018-12-25","seg1_from_code":"YUL","seg2_from_code":"YUL","seg3_from_code":"YUL","seg4_from_code":"YUL","num_adults":"1","num_children":"0","num_infants":"0","num_infants_lap":"0","seat_class":"Economy","seg1_from":"CWB","seg1_to":"YUL","campaign":"1","search_id":"81b68b249dcb5e09a55fea4bedaac660","flexible_search_id":"81b68b249dcb5e09a55fea4bedaac660"};
      payload.email = $(emailInputId).val();
      payload.source = $(parentContainerId + ' button.fare-alert-btn').data('source');
      payload.pid = $(parentContainerId + ' input[name="flight-package"]').val();
      fareAlert.subscribe(payload);
    }
